	color = { 6 95 78 }
	#landless = yes
	always_follows_primary_heir = yes
	definite_form = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = culture:sirrandrai
			}
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
}

	color = { 0 0 40 }
			  
	capital = c_mispir

	cultural_names = {
		name_list_dunedain = cn_otsonore
		name_list_ranger = cn_otsonore
		name_list_nandorin = cn_dorlaurmet
		
		name_list_seven_lands = cn_thani_hazad_native
		name_list_southern_apysaic = cn_thani_hazad_native
		name_list_nafarati = cn_thani_hazad_native
	}

	can_create = {
		custom_tooltip = { 
			text = struggle_thani_hazad_has_ended_trigger
			NOT = { exists = struggle:thani_hazad_struggle }
		}
